--- Commit Message ---
LU-10606 hsm: store HSM xattr as a basic layout

A closer coupling between the HSM archive state and Lustre File
Level Redundancy (FLR) can make PCC and HSM management more
consistent with the management of other replicas in the file
system. Stroing HSM as a layout (FLR component of the file) can
obtain the following benefits:
- Consolidate the HSM with PFL/FLR/composite layouts to give a
  flexibility way to combine these features;
- Migration, FLR mirroring resync and HSM data movement all
  could be done through a user-space copytool;
- Allow multiple HSM copies (e.g. Tape, S3, another POSIX copy),
  which would also be useful for file versioning, flexible
  archiving;
- Allow PCC-RW mirror to be kept at the same as regular file
  mirror, by marking the regular file mirror(s) stale instead of
  releasing them;
- Possibly keep partial file components in the HSM, for limiting
  restore extents or for PFL layouts.

This patch implements the basic framework to store HSM xattr as
a basic layout component.

Test-Parameters: clientcount=3 testlist=sanity-pcc,sanity-hsm

--- Message (Ben Evans, 2020-07-17 14:06:36.000000000) ---
Patch Set 2: Code-Review-1

(2 comments)

This needs an update to move existing HSM installations to the new format.

--- Message (Qian Yingjin, 2020-07-17 15:23:11.000000000) ---
Patch Set 2:

I agree we should move the old HSM xattr in the old Lustre system into the new format as a basic layout component especially during system upgrade.
But check this when get HSM information in XXX_hsm_attr_get may be too expensive...
Should we develop a tool to transform the old HSM xattr into the new format when the system upgrades?

--- Message (Ben Evans, 2020-07-17 15:29:49.000000000) ---
Patch Set 2:

> I agree we should move the old HSM xattr in the old Lustre system
 > into the new format as a basic layout component especially during
 > system upgrade.
 > But check this when get HSM information in XXX_hsm_attr_get may be
 > too expensive...
 > Should we develop a tool to transform the old HSM xattr into the
 > new format when the system upgrades?

I'd prefer that it be done in-line, because we can't guarantee that a customer has run the update tools on all their MDTs (and they finished correctly and...).  Check for the new layout first, then check for the old if it fails?  That way the cost is only paid once per file, not every time.

--- Message (Andreas Dilger, 2020-07-19 12:11:56.000000000) ---
Patch Set 2:

Ben, because old clients cannot understand this new layout component, I don't think we can make it the default immediately. First we need a patch to add the handling of this component type, and also fix FLR/clients to ignore components the do not understand, if they can still read/write the mirror without it.  The MDS would mark the other unknown mirrors stale if there is a usable copy.

That should be backported to 2.12 at least, to maximize compatibility.

This will also be useful eg. for FLR-EC access by older clients (though they would not be able to regenerate parity if a stripe was down).

After that, the admin would have a runtime option to decide whether to convert the HSM xattr to the new layout or not.

--- Message (Andreas Dilger, 2020-07-19 20:30:33.000000000) ---
Patch Set 2:

> > I agree we should move the old HSM xattr in the old Lustre system
 > > into the new format as a basic layout component especially during
 > > system upgrade.
 > > But check this when get HSM information in XXX_hsm_attr_get may
 > be
 > > too expensive...
 > > Should we develop a tool to transform the old HSM xattr into the
 > > new format when the system upgrades?

If there is a tool to do this, it could be done as part of LFSCK, so that it can be done when the filesystem is mounted.  Having a special-case offline tool is not very useful for users.

 > I'd prefer that it be done in-line, because we can't guarantee that
 > a customer has run the update tools on all their MDTs (and they
 > finished correctly and...).  Check for the new layout first, then
 > check for the old if it fails?  That way the cost is only paid once
 > per file, not every time.

In the distant past (i.e. at 1.0) we updated layouts from some obsolete format (layout saved in body of MDT inode) to the lov_magic_v1 xattr we still have today.  Essentially, it checked for the new format first (since all new files used the new format), but if not present it checked for the old format and then rewrote the layout in the new format.  At that point, the upgrade "tool" was to just use the filesystem for some time, or run "ls -lR" (or equivalent) for the whole filesystem.

That said, we *don't* want to force the new format xattr until there is compatibility code that would return the HSM component to userspace if the "trusted.hsm" xattr is read, for compatibility with old HSM copytools.

--- Message (Andreas Dilger, 2020-07-19 20:36:07.000000000) ---
Patch Set 2:

I think for 2.14 (and backport to 2.12.6), the first step is the ability for clients and MDS to skip unknown component types in an FLR mirror (LU-13602), if possible.  Then, once we decide on the final layout format (type of foreign layout vs. separate LOV_MAGIC_HSM) we might include only the support for _reading_ such xattrs as "trusted.hsm" into 2.14 (if change is small), and add the rest of the code for creating/modifying such components until after 2.14.

--- Message (Ben Evans, 2020-07-20 13:39:52.000000000) ---
Patch Set 3:

> That said, we *don't* want to force the new format xattr until
 > there is compatibility code that would return the HSM component to
 > userspace if the "trusted.hsm" xattr is read, for compatibility
 > with old HSM copytools.

Just on this point, I don't think the copytool can parse out the HSM xattr, since the data structure is all on the MDT.  What is needed from those xattrs, the copytool gets sent when the action begins.  Otherwise, it's things like data versions and archive numbers and a few flags.

--- Message (Andreas Dilger, 2021-01-29 22:19:23.000000000) ---
Patch Set 11: Code-Review-1

(4 comments)

I think this is starting to look good, but it is missing important compatibility code for working with existing MDT filesystems that have HSM xattrs, and older clients that may be trying to access/modify the HSM xattrs themselves.

We can't remove all of the existing HSM xattr support until after the HSM xattr-in-layout code has been around for a few releases, and there has been a chance to convert existing xattrs over to the new format.  This version still needs to allow accessing the HSM attrs via the old interface, even if they are stored as part of the LOV layout xattr.

--- Message (Andreas Dilger, 2021-01-29 22:23:08.000000000) ---
Patch Set 11:

This patch failed all of the sanity-hsm tests and some of the sanity tests related to file layouts.  It would be good to add test sessions to this patch to ensure that interop is working properly:

 Test-Parameters: testlist=sanity-hsm clientversion=2.12.6
 Test-Parameters: testlist=sanity-hsm serverversion=2.12.6

When those sessions are passing then we know the interop is correct.

--- Message (Aurelien Degremont, 2021-02-12 11:06:13.000000000) ---
Patch Set 11:

(2 comments)

I agree implementing the HSM state as a FLR flags is a good move.
I like this idea.

Reviewing this patch is hard as it is huge and the commit message is focused on explaining WHY we are doing rather than HOW it is implemented. It is better to consolidate the WHY in the JIRA ticket, potentially summarizing this a bit in the patch, but mostly explaining what changes are made and how these changes are working in the commit message.

Additionally, this patch is big and will have lots of difficulties to avoid conflicts and land easily. It will be very helpful if you can split it into smaller pieces. That would help reviewing, understanding the different changes, backport them to LTS if needed for compatibility.

--- Message (Etienne AUJAMES, 2024-01-24 11:40:17.000000000) ---
Patch Set 21:

> Maybe, this was an existing bug: I never played with FLR and HSM before.

Yes, sound like it. I tested the following fix on the kernel side of the copytool:

diff --git a/lustre/llite/dir.c b/lustre/llite/dir.c
index 253fbf7..f123965 100644
--- a/lustre/llite/dir.c
+++ b/lustre/llite/dir.c
@@ -1060,7 +1060,8 @@ static int ll_ioc_copy_end(struct super_block *sb, struct 
                        GOTO(progress, rc = PTR_ERR(inode));
                }
 
-               rc = ll_data_version(inode, &data_version, LL_DV_RD_FLUSH);
+               rc = ll_data_version(inode, &data_version,
+                                    LL_DV_RD_FLUSH | LL_DV_SZ_UPDATE);

This is working now with the small fix.
I am not sure if we should fix this here, but since this patch mixes FLR and HSM, I am not against it.

Patch Set 21: Code-Review-1

I found an important bug, hsm layout does not seems to be correctly sync on disk:

I was troubleshooting a bug in "lfs getstripe -v":

[root@client client]# ~eaujames/lustre-release/lustre/utils/lfs hsm_state test3
test3: (0x0000000d) released exists archived, archive_id:1                          
[root@client client]# ~eaujames/lustre-release/lustre/utils/.libs/lfs getstripe -v test3                    
test3                                                                                                       
composite_header:                                                                                           
  lcm_magic:         0x0BD60BD0                                                                             
  lcm_size:          152                                                                                    
  lcm_flags:         0                                                                                      
  lcm_layout_gen:    2                                                                                      
  lcm_mirror_count:  1                                                                                      
  lcm_entry_count:   1                                                                                      
components:                                                                                                 
  - lcme_id:             131074                                                                             
    lcme_mirror_id:      2                                                                                  
    lcme_flags:          init                                                                               
    lcme_extent.e_start: 0                                                                                  
    lcme_extent.e_end:   EOF                                                                                
    lcme_offset:         80                                                                                 
    lcme_size:           72                                                                                 
    sub_layout:                                                                                             
      lhm_magic:         0x0BD70BD0                                                                         
      lhm_pattern:       hsm                                                                                
      lhm_length:        56                                                                                 
      lhm_type:          0x00000001 (posix)                                                                 
      lhm_flags:         exists,released,archived,0xd                                                       
      lhm_archive_id:    8589935619                    <-----
      lhm_archive_ver:   4299161600                                                                         
      lhm_archive_uuid:  ''                                                                                 

The lhm_archive_id/lhm_archive_ver are not correct.

But the issue is not on the getattr path:

[root@mds1 ~]# debugfs -c -R 'ea_get -f /tmp/lov.bin /ROOT/test3 trusted.lov' /dev/mapper/mds1_flakey
[root@mds1 ~]# xxd -g4 /tmp/lov.bin
0000000: d00bd60b 98000000 02000000 00000100  ................
0000010: 00000000 00000000 00000000 00000000  ................
0000020: 02000200 10000000 00000000 00000000  ................
0000030: ffffffff ffffffff 50000000 48000000  ........P...H...
0000040: 00000000 00000000 00000000 00000000  ................
0000050: d00bd70b 38000000 01000000 0d000000  ....8...........
0000060: 03040000 02000000 00004000 01000000  ..........@.....
0000070: 00000000 00000000 00000000 00000000  ................
0000080: 00000000 00000000 00000000 00000000  ................
0000090: 00000000 00000000                    ........

The same values are found directly on the disk:
d00bd70b: foreign magic layout
38000000: 56 lhm_length
01000000: 1 lhm_type
0d000000: 0xd lhm_flags
03040000 02000000: 0x0200000403 (8589935619) 
00004000 01000000: 0x0100400000 (4299161600)

This is confirmed by cleaning the MDT cache:

[root@mds1 ~]# umount /dev/mapper/mds1_flakey 
[root@mds1 ~]# mount -t lustre /dev/mapper/mds1_flakey /media/lustrefs/client-mds1/
[root@client client]# ~eaujames/lustre-release/lustre/utils/lfs hsm_state test3
test3: (0x0000000d) released exists archived, archive_id:1027

1027 = 0x403
